                var showctTimer;
                $(".now_city").hover(function () {
                    $(this).addClass("now_citycur");
                    clearTimeout(showctTimer);
                    var pos = $(this).offset();
                    $(".city-wrap").show().css({ left: pos.left, top: pos.top+24, position: "absolute" });
                    if(!isChangeCity){
                        Area.change();
                        isChangeCity=true;
                    }
                }, function () {
                    if (Cookie.Get("ischecked") == "1") {
                        showctTimer = setTimeout(function () {
                            $(".city-wrap").hide();
                            $(".now_city").removeClass("now_citycur");
                        }, 300);
                    }
                });
                $(".city-wrap").hover(function () { clearTimeout(showctTimer); }, function () {
                    if (Cookie.Get("ischecked") == "1") {$(".city-wrap").hide();}
                    $(".now_city").removeClass("now_citycur");
                });
            });
            if(Cookie.Get("ischecked")==null && Cookie.ISCookie()){
                $(".city-wrap").show().css({left:"50%",top:"50%",marginLeft:"-250px",marginTop:"-135px", position: "fixed" });
                mark("show");
                Area.change();
                $(".city-wrap a.close").click(function(){//直接点关闭则设置IP定位到的城市
                    var AreaData=Area.cityData;
                    if (AreaData!= null) {
                        var d2 = AreaData;
                        for(var i=0;i<d2.length;i++){
                            if(d2[i].id==3364){

                                );
                            }
                        }

                        Area.init(3363,3364,3365,"全国","全国","全国",false);
                }
                Area.setCity();
                });
                }

                function closeCt(){
                    $(".city-wrap").hide()

                <script>
                    /*hoverShow($(".quick-recharge-btn"), $(".quick-recharge"));*/
                    function closeQuickRecharge() {
                        $(".quick-recharge").hide();
                    }
                    var ajaxFlowFlag = null;
                    $(".quick-recharge-btn").mouseover(function () {
                        $(".quick-recharge").show();
                        if (userMobile) {
                            $("#chongNum").val(userMobile);
                            checkRecharge();
                        }
                    });
                    $(document).click(function () {
                        $(".quick-recharge").hide();
                    });
                    $(".quick-recharge").click(function (e) {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                    });

                    function setType(type) {
                        if (type == 1) {
                            $("#sePrice").show(); $("#seFlow,#seFlowArea").hide();
                            $("#seFlowArea").parent().siblings("dt").html("面值：");
                        }
                        if (type == 2) {
                            $("#sePrice").hide(); $("#seFlow,#seFlowArea").show();
                            $("#seFlowArea").parent().siblings("dt").html("流量：");
                            $("#rePri").html("");
                        }
                    }
                    function checkRecharge() {
                        var num = $.trim($("#chongNum").val());
                        var Amount = $("#sePrice").val();
                        if (!IsMobile(num)) {
                            layer.tips("请检查号码输入是否正确！", $("#chongNum"));
                            return false;
                        }
                        $("#yys,#rePri").html('<img style="vertical-align:middle;" src="http://img2.ch999img.com/images/loading.gif" />');
                        if ($("input[name=type]:checked").val() == 1) {
                                /*充话费*/
                                $.post("/recharge.aspx", { act: 'actPrice', amount: Amount, phone: num }, function (rsp) {
                                    if (rsp.name.indexOf("请检查") != -1) {
                                        layer.tips(rsp.name, $("#chongNum"));
                                        $("#yys").html("");
                                    } else { $("#yys").html(rsp.name); }
                                    $("#rePri").html("￥" + rsp.price);
                                }, "json");

                        } else if ($("input[name=type]:checked").val() == 2) {
                                if (ajaxFlowFlag) {
                                    ajaxFlowFlag.abort();
                                } else {
                                    ajaxFlowFlag = $.post("/recharge.aspx", { act: 'productList', phone: $.trim($("#chongNum").val()) }, function (rsp) {
                                        if (rsp.status == 1) {
                                            var data = rsp.data;
                                            if (data.length < 1) {
                                                layer.tips("很抱歉，该号码暂不支持流量充值！", $("#chongNum"));
                                                return false;
                                            }
                                            $("#seFlowArea option").show();
                                            $("#seFlow").html(template("chongTmpl", rsp.data)).show();
                                            if ($("#seFlow option[data-prodscope=0]").length < 1) { $("#seFlowArea option[value=0]").hide(); }
                                            if ($("#seFlow option[data-prodscope=1]").length < 1) { $("#seFlowArea option[value=1]").hide(); }

                                            $("#rePri").html("￥" + (parseInt(data[0].prodOfficialPrice) / 100).toFixed(2));
                                            $("#yys").html(data[0].prodName.replace(/\d*M.*/gi, ""));
                                        } else {
                                            $("#yys").html("");
                                            layer.tips(rsp.msg, $("#chongNum"));
                                        }
                                    }, "json");
                                }
                                Amount = $("#seFlow").val();
                                /*充流量  prodScope0为本地 1为全国*/
                                if ($("#seFlow option:selected").length < 1) { $("#seFlow").hide(); $("#yys,#rePri").html(""); return false; }
                                var p = $("#seFlow option:selected").attr("data-price");
                                $("#rePri").html("￥" + (parseInt(p) / 100).toFixed(2));
                                $("#yys").html("");
                            }
                        }
                        $("#chongNum").keyup(function (e) {
                            var num = $.trim($(this).val());
                            if (num.length == 11) {
                                checkRecharge();
                            }
                        });
                        $(document).on("change", "#sePrice,#seFlow", function () { checkRecharge(); });
                        $(document).on("change", "#seFlowArea", function () {
                            /*充流量  prodScope0为本地 1为全国*/
                            $("#seFlowArea option").prop("style", "");
                            var dom = $("#seFlow option[data-prodscope=" + $(this).val() + "]");
                            if (dom.length < 1) { $("#seFlow").hide(); } else {
                                $("#seFlow").show();
                                dom.show().siblings("[data-prodscope!=" + $(this).val() + "]").hide();
                            }
                        });
                        function submitRecharge() {
                            var num = $.trim($("#chongNum").val());
                            if ($("input[name=type]:checked").val() == 1) {
                                var Amount = $("#sePrice").val();
                                window.location.href = "/Recharge.aspx?type=1&act=tobeSure&phone=" + num + "&amount=" + Amount;
                            } else if ($("input[name=type]:checked").val() == 2) {
                                var curDom = $("#seFlow option:selected");
                                window.location.href = "/Recharge.aspx?type=2&phone=" + num + "&prodid=" + curDom.val() + "&prodparvalue=" + curDom.text() + "&prodscope=" + curDom.attr("data-prodscope") + "&price=" + curDom.attr("data-price");
                            } else { layer.tips("信息提交失败，请重试！", $("#chongNum")); }
                        }
                    </script>

<script>

    $("#rightCartBox").css({ height: $(window).height() + "px" });
    $(document).on("click", "#rightCart", function () {
        if ($("#rightCartBox1").width() > 10) {
            $("#rightCartBox1").animate({ width: "0" }, 500);
        } else {
            cartN.loadCarInfo();
            $("#rightCartBox1").animate({ width: "280px" }, 500);
        }
    });
    $(document).on("click", "#rightCartBox1 .close", function () {
        $("#rightCart").trigger("click");
    });
    $(window).resize(function () { $("#rightCartBox").css({ height: $(window).height() + "px" }); });

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    if ($(".shop_scollbox li").length <= 3) {
        $(".turn_btn").hide();
    } else {
        crossRoller($(".shop_scoller"));
    }
    hoverShow($("#wsq_menu"), $("#wsq_ma"));
    $(".scrolltop").backToTop();
    /*发送店铺短信*/
    $(".shop_scollbox a[name=sendSMS],.seo_dianpu a[name=sendSMS]").click(function () {
        var mes = "", self = $(this);
        if (self.parents(".seo_dianpu").length > 0) {
            $(this).parent().siblings("p").each(function () {
                mes += $(this).text() + '\n';
            });
        } else {
            $(this).siblings("p").each(function () {
                mes += $(this).text() + '\n';
            });
        }
        var ztid = $(this).attr("id");
        if (ztid == "") {
            changeShowtip("无店面id", $(this));
        }
        sendToPhone(mes, ztid, 1);
    });
    /*图挂了*/
    var allimg = document.getElementsByTagName('img');
    for (var i = 0; i < allimg.length; i++) {
        allimg[i].onerror = function () { this.src = 'http://img2.ch999img.com/images/wutu.gif'; };
        }
</script>

            $(".floor_tit b").each(function () {
                var the = $(this);
                var title = the.html();
                if (title.indexOf("5") != -1) {
                    the.html(title.replace(/5/g, "2"));
                }
                if (title.indexOf("2") != -1) {
                    the.html(title.replace(/2/g, "3"));
                }
                if (title.indexOf("3") != -1) {
                    the.html(title.replace(/3/g, "4"));
                }
                if (title.indexOf("4") != -1) {
                    the.html(title.replace(/4/g, "5"));
                }
            });
        }

        showTag($(".flpro_list li"));

        $(".bk_box ul li").last().css({ border: 0 });
        $(".floor_paihang").each(function () {
            $(this).find("li").last().css({ border: 0 });
        });

        $(".side_tab a").mouseover(function () {
            $(this).addClass("cur").siblings().removeClass("cur");
            var i = $(this).index();
            $(".trytab").eq(i).show().siblings(".trytab").hide();
        });

        var floorTabTimer;
        $(".floor_tab a").hover(function () {
            clearTimeout(floorTabTimer);
            var the = $(this);
            var i = the.index();
            var showObj = the.parents(".floor").find(".floor_pro");
            floorTabTimer = setTimeout(function () {
                the.addClass("cur").siblings().removeClass("cur");
                showObj.eq(i).show().siblings().hide();
            }, 200);
        }, function () {
            clearTimeout(floorTabTimer);
        });
        $(".floor_ad").each(function () {
            var the = $(this);
            var fla = the.find(".flad_a");
            var a = fla.find("span");
            var b = the.find("li");
            autoBanner(a, b, "cur", 3500);
        });

        var windowWidth = $(window).width();

        for (var i = 0; i < floor.length; i++) {
            /*if (Cookie.Get("dtad")) {*/
                floorTop.push(floor.eq(i).offset().top);
            /*} else {
                floorTop.push(floor.eq(i).offset().top + 70);
            }*/
        }

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= floorTop[0] - 300 && $(window).scrollTop() <= floorTop[floorTop.length - 1] + 50) {
                $(".elevator").show().css({ left: ($(window).width() - 1280) / 2 });
            } else {
                $(".elevator").hide();
            }

            for (var j = 0; j < floorTop.length; j++) {
                if ($(window).scrollTop() >= floorTop[j] + 20) {
                    $(".elevator a").eq(j + 1).addClass("cur").siblings().removeClass("cur");
                } else if ($(window).scrollTop() <= floorTop[0]) {
                    $(".elevator a").eq(0).addClass("cur").siblings().removeClass("cur");
                }
            }
        });
        $(".elevator a").click(function () {
            var i = $(this).index();
            $("html,body").animate({ scrollTop: floorTop[i] }, 300);
        });
